Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n93\t    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n94\t    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n95\t    \"\"\"\n96\t    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n97\t    if match is None:\n98\t        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n99\t\n100\t    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n101\t\n102\t    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n103\t    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n104\t    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n105\t        line = line.strip()\n106\t        if \":\" in line:\n107\t            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n108\t            if key:\n109\t                found_keys.add(key)\n110\t\n111\t    for field in required_fields:\n112\t        if field not in found_keys:\n113\t            return (\n114\t                False,\n115\t                f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\",\n116\t            )\n117\t\n118\t    return True, None\n119\t"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_0196RrqSMzAo3VXfkqVFHhj6","session_id":"1baabfdc-1ec4-4e9d-87de-d3d40aac9266","uuid":"610bad16-1d88-4fad-9beb-7b9c1149110b","timestamp":"2026-04-12T21:07:26.414Z"}

All types here are generic pipeline\nprimitives that both consumers extend.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Callable, Literal, Optional\n\n\nclass StepStatus(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Lifecycle status of a single pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    PENDING = \"PENDING\"\n    PASS = \"PASS\"\n    FAIL = \"FAIL\"\n    TIMEOUT = \"TIMEOUT\"\n    CANCELLED = \"CANCELLED\"\n    SKIPPED = \"SKIPPED\"\n\n    @property\n    def is_terminal(self) -> bool:\n        return self in (\n            StepStatus.PASS,\n            StepStatus.FAIL,\n            StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n            StepStatus.SKIPPED,\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def is_success(self) -> bool:\n        return self == StepStatus.PASS\n\n    @property\n    def is_failure(self) -> bool:\n        return self in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n\n\nclass GateMode(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Gating behavior for pipeline steps.\n\n    BLOCKING: Step must pass before the next step can begin (default).\n    TRAILING: Step runs but does not block subsequent steps; failures\n              are evaluated after a grace period.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    BLOCKING = \"BLOCKING\"\n    TRAILING = \"TRAILING\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    \"\"\"Pure Python check applied to file content. self.started_at).total_seconds()\n\n\nclass DeliverableKind(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Classification of deliverable type for decomposition and analysis.\"\"\"\n\n    IMPLEMENT = \"implement\"\n    VERIFY = \"verify\"\n    INVARIANT_CHECK = \"invariant_check\"\n    FMEA_TEST = \"fmea_test\"\n    GUARD_TEST = \"guard_test\"\n    CONTRACT_TEST = \"contract_test\"\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_str(cls, value: str) -> DeliverableKind:\n        \"\"\"Parse a string into a DeliverableKind, raising ValueError on unknown.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return cls(value)\n        except ValueError:\n            valid = \", \".join(k.value for k in cls)\n            raise ValueError(\n                f\"Unknown deliverable kind: {value!r}. Valid kinds: {valid}\"\n            )\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Deliverable:\n    \"\"\"A single deliverable within a pipeline step or roadmap task.\n\n    Attributes:\n        id: Unique identifier (e.g. 'D-0001', 'D-0001.a').\n        description: Human-readable description of what this deliverable produces.\n        kind: Classification for decomposition passes. Defaults to 'implement'\n              for backward compatibility with pre-extension deliverables.\n        metadata: Attachment point for analytical passes (M2-M4). Defaults to\n                  empty dict. Round-trip serializable.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    id: str\n    description: str\n    kind: DeliverableKind = DeliverableKind.IMPLEMENT\n    metadata: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n    def to_dict(self) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Serialize to a dict for JSON round-trip.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"id\": self.id,\n            \"description\": self.description,\n            \"kind\": self.kind.value,\n            \"metadata\": self.metadata,\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data: dict) -> Deliverable:\n        \"\"\"Deserialize from a dict. Pre-extension dicts without 'kind' default to 'implement'.\"\"\"\n        kind_str = data.get(\"kind\", \"implement\")\n        return cls(\n            id=data[\"id\"],\n            description=data[\"description\"],\n            kind=DeliverableKind.from_str(kind_str),\n            metadata=data.get(\"metadata\", {}),\n        )\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass PipelineConfig:\n    \"\"\"Configuration shared by both sprint and roadmap pipelines.\"\"\"\n\n    work_dir: Path = field(default_factory=lambda: Path(\".\"))\n    dry_run: bool = False\n    max_turns: int = 100\n    model: str = \"\"\n    permission_flag: str = \"--dangerously-skip-permissions\"\n    debug: bool = False\n    grace_period: int = 0\n```\n\n### Key base types from this file\n\n- `PipelineConfig` fields:\n  - NFR-007: No sprint/roadmap imports.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\n\n\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    # EXEMPT: always passes\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must exist\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must be non-empty\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT stops here\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: minimum line count\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: YAML frontmatter fields\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(\n            content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file\n        )\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    # STANDARD stops here\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STRICT: semantic checks\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            result = check.check_fn(content)\n            if result is not True:\n                detail = result if isinstance(result, str) else check.failure_message\n                return (\n                    False,\n                    f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {detail}\",\n                )\n\n    return True, None\n\n\n_FRONTMATTER_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"^---[ \\t]*\\n((?:[ \\t]*\\w[\\w\\s]*:.*\\n)+)---[ \\t]*$\",\n    re.MULTILINE,\n)\n\n\ndef _check_frontmatter(\n    content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path\n) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Extract and validate YAML frontmatter fields.\n\n    Uses regex with re.MULTILINE to discover frontmatter anywhere in the\n    document (not just byte 0), allowing conversational preamble before the\n    ``---`` delimiters.  Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n    \"\"\"\n    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n    if match is None:\n        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n\n    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n\n    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" in line:\n            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n            if key:\n                found_keys.add(key)\n\n    for field in required_fields:\n        if field not in found_keys:\n            return (\n                False,\n                f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\",\n            )\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\n### Exact interfaces requested\n\n- `GateCriteria` is imported from models and has fields:\n  - `required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]`\n  - `min_lines: int`\n  - `enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"`\n  - `semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None`\n\n- `gate_passed()` signature:\n  - `gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]`\n\n- `_check_frontmatter()` signature:\n  - `_check_frontmatter(content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path) -> tuple[bool, str | None]`\n\n### Gate behavior\n- `EXEMPT`: always passes\n- `LIGHT`: file exists + non-empty\n- `STANDARD`: LIGHT + min lines + required YAML frontmatter fields\n- `STRICT`: STANDARD + semantic checks\n\n---\n\n## 3. `src/superclaude/cli/prd/` existence and contents\n\nChecked via glob and directory listing.\n\nResult:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/prd/` does **not exist**\n- No files found under that path\n\nThis aligns Pre-extension dicts without 'kind' default to 'implement'.\"\"\"\n        kind_str = data.get(\"kind\", \"implement\")\n        return cls(\n            id=data[\"id\"],\n            description=data[\"description\"],\n            kind=DeliverableKind.from_str(kind_str),\n            metadata=data.get(\"metadata\", {}),\n        )\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass PipelineConfig:\n    \"\"\"Configuration shared by both sprint and roadmap pipelines.\"\"\"\n\n    work_dir: Path = field(default_factory=lambda: Path(\".\"))\n    dry_run: bool = False\n    max_turns: int = 100\n    model: str = \"\"\n    permission_flag: str = \"--dangerously-skip-permissions\"\n    debug: bool = False\n    grace_period: int = 0\n```\n\n### Key base types from this file\n\n- `PipelineConfig` fields:\n  - NFR-007: No sprint/roadmap imports.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\n\n\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    # EXEMPT: always passes\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must exist\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must be non-empty\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT stops here\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: minimum line count\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: YAML frontmatter fields\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(\n            content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file\n        )\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    # STANDARD stops here\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STRICT: semantic checks\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            result = check.check_fn(content)\n            if result is not True:\n                detail = result if isinstance(result, str) else check.failure_message\n                return (\n                    False,\n                    f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {detail}\",\n                )\n\n    return True, None\n\n\n_FRONTMATTER_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"^---[ \\t]*\\n((?:[ \\t]*\\w[\\w\\s]*:.*\\n)+)---[ \\t]*$\",\n    re.MULTILINE,\n)\n\n\ndef _check_frontmatter(\n    content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path\n) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Extract and validate YAML frontmatter fields.\n\n    Uses regex with re.MULTILINE to discover frontmatter anywhere in the\n    document (not just byte 0), allowing conversational preamble before the\n    ``---`` delimiters.  Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n    \"\"\"\n    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n    if match is None:\n        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n\n    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n\n    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" in line:\n            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n            if key:\n                found_keys.add(key)\n\n    for field in required_fields:\n        if field not in found_keys:\n            return (\n                False,\n                f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\",\n            )\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\n### Exact interfaces requested\n\n- `GateCriteria` is imported from models and has fields:\n  - `required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]`\n  - `min_lines: int`\n  - `enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"`\n  - `semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None`\n\n- `gate_passed()` signature:\n  - `gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]`\n\n- `_check_frontmatter()` signature:\n  - `_check_frontmatter(content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path) -> tuple[bool, str | None]`\n\n### Gate behavior\n- `EXEMPT`: always passes\n- `LIGHT`: file exists + non-empty\n- `STANDARD`: LIGHT + min lines + required YAML frontmatter fields\n- `STRICT`: STANDARD + semantic checks\n\n---\n\n## 3. `src/superclaude/cli/prd/` existence and Existing test patterns in `tests/cli/`\n\nOnly current file found:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/tests/cli/test_tdd_extract_prompt.py`\n\n### Full contents read\nI won’t paste the whole 250-line file again unless you want it verbatim, but I did read it fully. Here are the conventions it establishes:\n\n#### Structure conventions\n- Module docstring at top\n- `from __future__ import annotations`\n- imports grouped cleanly\n- `pytest` fixture near top\n- tests organized in `class Test...:` groups with docstrings\n- test names use `test_<behavior>` style\n- assertions are direct and specific\n- comments used sparingly but clearly\n\n#### Concrete examples\n- Fixture pattern:\n  - `@pytest.fixture`\n  - helper fixture returns `Path` objects written under `tmp_path`\n- Grouped classes:\n  - `class TestBuildExtractPromptTdd:`\n  - `class TestBuildExtractPromptUnchanged:`\n  - `class TestRoadmapConfigDefaults:`\n  - `class TestTasklistValidateConfigDefaults:`\n  - `class TestAutoDetection:`\n  - `class TestTddInputValidation:`\n- Assertions:\n  - `assert section in result`\n  - `assert detect_input_type(tdd) == \"tdd\"`\n  - `assert config.tdd_file is None`\n\n#### Likely conventions for future `tests/cli/prd/`\nBased on this file and the release spec:\n- use `pytest`\n- use `tmp_path` fixtures for filesystem cases\n- group tests by function or behavior in classes\n- test names stay descriptive and explicit\n- validate exact strings and enum/property behavior directly\n- no heavy abstraction in tests\n\n---\n\n## 7. Source release spec section 4.6 Implementation Order\n\n```text\n1.  models.py          -- zero internal deps, defines all domain types\n2.  gates.py           -- depends on pipeline.models only\n3.  inventory.py       -- depends on models (file discovery utilities)\n4.  filtering.py       -- depends on inventory (partitioning, gap compilation)\n5.  prompts.py         -- depends on models (prompt builders read config + files)\n6.  config.py          -- depends on models, inventory (CLI arg -> PrdConfig)\n7.  monitor.py         -- depends on models (NDJSON signal parsing)\n8.  process.py         -- depends on pipeline.process, models (ClaudeProcess extension)\n9.  logging_.py        -- depends on models (JSONL + Markdown logging)\n10. diagnostics.py     -- depends on models (failure classification, resume output)\n11. tui.py             -- depends on models, monitor (Rich live dashboard)\n12. executor.py        -- depends on all above (main execution loop)\n13. commands.py        -- depends on config, executor (Click CLI group)\n14. __init__.py        -- depends on commands (package exports)\n\nParallelization: steps 3-6 are independent of 7-10 and could be implemented concurrently.\n```\n\nThis is useful for understanding intended extension layering.\n\n---\n\n## 7c. Structure\n\n> **Note:** This section is reference documentation. The synthesis agents produce sections that are assembled into this format.\n\n```markdown\n---\n[frontmatter from template]\n---\n\n# [Product Name] - Product Requirements Document (PRD)\n\n> HOW TO USE THIS DOCUMENT: [preamble blockquote]\n\n---\n\n## Document Information\nProject specifics table: Product Name, Product Owner, Engineering Lead, Design Lead, Stakeholders, Status, Target Release, Last Updated, Review Cadence.\n\n## Table of Contents\n[Generated from section headers]\n\n---\n\n## 1. Executive Summary\n2-3 paragraph summary with Key Success Metrics.\n\n## 2. Problem Statement\nCore problem, why existing solutions fall short, market opportunity.\n\n## 3. Background & Strategic Fit\nWhy now, company objective alignment, strategic bets.\n\n## 4. Product Vision\nOne-sentence vision statement with expansion.\n\n## 5. Business Context\nMarket opportunity (TAM/SAM/SOM), business objectives, KPIs.\n\n## 6. Jobs To Be Done (JTBD)\nPrimary jobs in When/I want/So that format, related jobs table.\n\n## 7. User Personas\nPrimary, secondary, tertiary personas with attribute tables; anti-personas.\n\n## 8. Value Proposition Canvas\nCustomer profile, value map (pain relievers + gain creators), fit assessment.\n\n## 9. Competitive Analysis\nCompetitive landscape table, feature comparison matrix, positioning statement, response plan.\n\n## 10. Assumptions & Constraints\nTechnical, business, and user assumptions with risk-if-wrong; constraints table.\n\n## 11. Dependencies\nExternal, internal, and cross-team dependency tables.\n\n## 12. Scope Definition\nIn scope, out of scope, permanently out of scope.\n\n## 13. Open Questions\nQuestion tracking table with owner, status, resolution.\n\n## 14. Technical Requirements\nArchitecture, performance, security, scalability, data & analytics requirements.\n\n## 15. Technology Stack\nBackend, frontend, infrastructure technology tables.\n\n## 16. User Experience Requirements\nOnboarding metrics, core user flows, accessibility, localization.\n\n## 17. Legal & Compliance Requirements\nRegulatory compliance, data privacy, terms & policies.\n\n## 18. Business Requirements\nMonetization strategy, pricing tiers, go-to-market, support requirements.\n\n## 19. Success Metrics & Measurement\nProduct, business, and technical metrics with targets and measurement frequency.\n\n## 20. Risk Analysis\nTechnical, business, and operational risk matrices with mitigations.\n\n## 21. Implementation Plan\nConsolidated delivery plan: 21.1 Epics, Features & Stories (epic summary, user stories with acceptance criteria), 21.2 Product Requirements (core features, RICE matrix), 21.3 Implementation Phasing, 21.4 Release Criteria & DoD, 21.5 Timeline & Milestones.\n\n## 22. Customer Journey Map\nJourney stages table, moments of truth.\n\n## 23. Error Handling & Edge Cases\nError categories, edge case scenarios, graceful degradation plan.\n\n## 24. User Interaction & Design\nWireframes/mockups table, design system checklist, prototype links.\n\n## 25. API Contract Examples\nKey endpoint request/response examples.\n\n## 26. Contributors & Collaboration\nContributor table, how to contribute guidelines.\n\n## 27. Related Resources\nCustomer research, technical docs, design assets, business documents.\n\n## 28. Maintenance & Ownership\nDocument ownership, review cadence, update process.\n\n## Appendices\nGlossary, Acronyms, Technical Architecture Diagrams, User Research Data, Financial Projections.\n\n## Document Approval\nApproval signature table.\n```\n\n---\n\n## Synthesis Mapping Table (Reference)\n\n> **Note:** This section is reference documentation. markers.\n    \"\"\"\n    patterns = [\n        (r\"\\bTODO\\b\", \"TODO\"),\n        (r\"\\bTBD\\b\", \"TBD\"),\n        (r\"\\bPLACEHOLDER\\b\", \"PLACEHOLDER\"),\n        (r\"\\[INSERT[^\\]]*\\]\", rf\"(?:^|\\n)\\s*\\*{{0,2}}{field_name}\\*{{0,2}}\\s*:\\s*\\S\",\n            re.IGNORECASE,\n        )\n        if not json_pat.search(content) and not md_pat.search(content):\n \"Technical Architecture\",\n    \"User Flows\",\n    \"Integration Points\",\n    \"Existing Documentation\",\n    \"Gap Analysis\",\n    \"Suggested Phases\",\n]\n\n\ndef _check_suggested_phases_detail(content: str) -> bool | str:\n    \"\"\"Check that the Suggested Phases section contains per-agent detail.\n\n    Expects at least one numbered or bulleted list item phase_headings = re.findall(\n        r\"(?:^|\\n)\\s*#{{1,4}}\\s+.*Phase\\s+\\d\", content, re.IGNORECASE\n    )\n    if len(phase_headings) < 2:\n        return f\"Expected multiple phase headings,     if phrase.lower() in item_text.lower():\n                violations.append(f\"'{phrase}' in: {item_text[:60]}\")\n    if violations:\n        return (\n            f\"Self-containment violations \"\"\"Build a SemanticCheck with crash-safe wrapper.\"\"\"\n    return SemanticCheck(\n        name=name,\n        check_fn=_safe_check(name, fn),\n        failure_message=failure_message,\n \"description\": match.group(1).strip(),\n            \"source_file\": source_file,\n        })\n\n    # Pattern 2: Items under Gap Analysis heading\n    gap_section = re.search(\n        r\"(?:^|\\n)\\s*#{{1,4}}\\s+(?:Gap\\s+Analysis|Gaps)\\s*\\n(.*?)(?=\\n\\s*#|\\Z)\",\n        content,\n        re.DOTALL | re.IGNORECASE,\n    )\n    if gap_section:\n        section_text = gap_section.group(1)\n        for line_match in re.finditer(\n            r\"^\\s*[-*]\\s+(.+)$\", section_text, re.MULTILINE\n        ):\n            desc = line_match.group(1).strip()\n            if desc and not desc.startswith(\"#\"):\n                gaps.append({\n                    \"description\": desc,\n                    \"source_file\": source_file,\n                })\n\n    return ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef merge_qa_partition_reports(reports: list[dict]) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Merge multiple QA partition reports with pessimistic verdict.\n\n    GAP-005: Overall verdict is FAIL if ANY partition reports FAIL.\n    Only returns PASS if ALL partitions pass.\n\n    Args:\n        reports: List of dicts, each with at ``partitions_passed``, ``partitions_failed``, and ``issues``.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not reports:\n        return {\n            \"verdict\": \"PASS\",\n            \"partition_count\": 0,\n            \"partitions_passed\": 0,\n            \"partitions_failed\": 0,\n            \"issues\": [],\n        }\n\n    all_issues: list[str] = []\n    passed = 0\n    failed = 0\n\n    for report in reports:\n        verdict = report.get(\"verdict\", \"FAIL\").upper()\n        if verdict == \"PASS\":\n            passed += 1\n        else:\n            failed += 1\n        issues = report.get(\"issues\", [])\n        all_issues.extend(issues)\n\n    return {\n        \"verdict\": \"FAIL\" if failed > 0 else \"PASS\",\n        \"partition_count\": len(reports),\n        \"partitions_passed\": passed,\n        \"partitions_failed\": failed,\n        \"issues\": all_issues,\n    }\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#
